List of 10,000 zillion numbers with Conway-Wechsler system

Written by Fish on February 14, 2023.

This page is a list of English names of -illion numbers up to 10,000th zillion (decillinillion), defined with the Conway-Wechsler system.

  • (S) means the short scale and (L) means the long scale.
  • ^ means " power to". Therefore 10^6 is 106.
  • n-th zillion can be accessed with appending #n to the URL. For example, #1234 for 1234th milliquattuortrigintaducentillion.

Here follows the list.

  • (1st) million = 10^6 (S), 10^6 (L)
  • (2nd) billion = 10^9 (S), 10^12 (L)
  • (3rd) trillion = 10^12 (S), 10^18 (L)
  • (4th) quadrillion = 10^15 (S), 10^24 (L)
  • (5th) quintillion = 10^18 (S), 10^30 (L)
  • (6th) sextillion = 10^21 (S), 10^36 (L)
  • (7th) septillion = 10^24 (S), 10^42 (L)
  • (8th) octillion = 10^27 (S), 10^48 (L)
  • (9th) nonillion = 10^30 (S), 10^54 (L)
  • (10th) decillion = 10^33 (S), 10^60 (L)
  • (11th) undecillion = 10^36 (S), 10^66 (L)
  • (12th) duodecillion = 10^39 (S), 10^72 (L)
  • (13th) tredecillion = 10^42 (S), 10^78 (L)
